company as defined in Rule 405 of the Securities Act of 1933 (&#167;230.405 of this chapter) or Rule 12b-2 of the Securities Exchange
Act of 1934 (&#167;240.12b-2 of this chapter).</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">Emerging growth company <span id="xdx_90D_edei--EntityEmergingGrowthCompany_c20230421__20230421_z4XCVuSjaL53"><ix:nonNumeric contextRef="From2023-04-21to2023-04-21" format="ixt:booleanfalse" name="dei:EntityEmergingGrowthCompany">&#9744;</ix:nonNumeric></span></p>

has elected not to use the extended transition period for complying with any new or revised financial accounting standards provided pursuant

    <!-- Field: /Page -->

<p style="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 9.35pt">Item 8.01 Other Events</p>

<p style="font: bold 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 9.35pt">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 0.25in">On April 21,
2023, Comcast Corporation (&#8220;Comcast&#8221;) notified The Bank of New York Mellon, as trustee and calculation agent, that it will
transition its outstanding Floating Rate Notes due 2024 (CUSIP 20030N CX7) (the &#8220;Notes&#8221;) from using three-month USD LIBOR
to the three-month CME Term SOFR Reference Rate as administered by CME Group Benchmark Administration, Ltd. (or any successor administrator
thereof) (&#8220;Term SOFR&#8221;) plus a tenor spread adjustment.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 0.25in">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 0.25in">In accordance with the terms of the Notes and
pursuant to the Adjustable Interest Rate (LIBOR) Act (the &#8220;LIBOR Act&#8221;) and the final rule adopted by the Board of Governors
of the Federal Reserve System (the &#8220;FRS Board&#8221;) that implements the LIBOR Act (the &#8220;LIBOR Rule&#8221;), Comcast, as
the determining person for the Notes, has determined that the FRS Board-selected benchmark replacement will replace USD LIBOR in the Notes
on and after the first London banking day after June 30, 2023. Such replacement will be effective for determinations that are made after
June 30, 2023 and will not affect any determinations made on or prior to such date under the terms of the Notes. The applicable tenor
spread adjustment, as set forth in the LIBOR Act and in the LIBOR Rule, is 0.26161%.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 0.25in">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 0.25in">A separate notice regarding the FRS Board-selected
benchmark replacement for the Notes will be sent to holders via the Depository Trust and Clearing Corporation. This Current Report on
Form 8-K does not constitute a notice to holders of the Notes regarding the Term SOFR transition.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 0.25in">&#160;</p>
